Converting Emoticons to text¶

In [23]:
data.to_csv('Checkpoints/Train_1.csv',index=False)
In [24]:
%%time
import emot
old_tweets = []
old_tweets = data['Tweet']
new_tweets = []
for tweet in tqdm(old_tweets):
    # text = data['Tweet'][91]
    the_tweet = ""
    text = tweet
    for i in text.split():
    #     print(i)
        ans = emot.emoticons(i)
    #     print(ans)
        if len(ans)==1:
#             print(i)
            the_tweet =the_tweet +i+" "
        else:
            if ans['flag']==False:
                the_tweet =the_tweet +i+" "
            elif ans['flag']==True:
                if len(emot.emoticons(i)['mean'])==0:
                    the_tweet =the_tweet+ i+" "
                else:
                    if(ans['value'][0]==i):
#                         print(ans['mean'])
                        the_tweet =the_tweet+ans['mean'][0]+" "
                    else:
                        the_tweet = the_tweet+i+" "
            else:
                continue
    new_tweets.append(the_tweet)
data['Tweet'] = new_tweets

%%time
noemojis = []
for x in tqdm(range(0,data.shape[0])):
    noemojis.append((emoji.demojize(data.iloc[x]['Tweet'])))
data['Tweet'] = noemojis
data['Tweet']=data['Tweet'].str.replace(":", " ",regex=False)
data['Tweet']=data['Tweet'].str.replace("_", " ",regex=False)

Deleting Mentions¶

In [32]:
%%time
removing_mentions = []
for x in tqdm(data['Tweet']):
    removing_mentions.append(' '.join(re.sub("(@[A-Za-z0-9]+)", " ", x).split()))
data['Tweet'] = removing_mentions

Converting the ticker names in ticker and Tweet column from $$ to $¶












In [34]:



    


data[data['ticker'].str.contains("$$",regex=False) & data['Tweet'].str.contains("$$",regex=False)]



    















    
Out[34]:











  
    

      
      Tweet
      Sentiment Score
      ticker
      date
      time
    

  
  
  






















In [35]:



    


list_of_double_dollars = data[data['ticker'].str.contains("$$",regex=False) & data['Tweet'].str.contains("$$",regex=False)].index
for x in list_of_double_dollars:
    data['Tweet'].iloc[x]=data['Tweet'].iloc[x].replace("$$", "$")
    data['ticker'].iloc[x]=data['ticker'].iloc[x].replace("$$", "$")
print(len(data[data['ticker'].str.contains("$$",regex=False) & data['Tweet'].str.contains("$$",regex=False)].index))

Accented Characters to Normal Characters¶












In [36]:



    


%%time
decoded_tweet = []
for i in tqdm(range(data.shape[0])):
    decoded_tweet.append(data['Tweet'][i].encode('utf-8').decode('utf-8','ignore'))
data['Tweet']=decoded_tweet

Remove Stopwords¶












In [47]:



    


import nltk
from nltk.tokenize.toktok import ToktokTokenizer
tokenizer = ToktokTokenizer()
stopword_list = nltk.corpus.stopwords.words('english')
# stopword_list.remove('no')
# stopword_list.remove('not')
def remove_stopwords(text):
    tokens = tokenizer.tokenize(text)
    tokens = [token.strip() for token in tokens]
    filtered_tokens = [token for token in tokens if token not in stopword_list]
    filtered_text = ' '.join(filtered_tokens)    
    return filtered_text



    













In [48]:



    


data['Tweet']=data['Tweet'].apply(remove_stopwords)



    













In [49]:

Lemmatization¶












In [50]:



    


from nltk.stem import WordNetLemmatizer
lemma = WordNetLemmatizer()
data['Tweet'] = data['Tweet'].apply(lambda x: " ".join([lemma.lemmatize(word,'v') for word in x.split()]))

Converting the sentiment score range to Positive Negative Neutral¶












In [52]:



    


negative_comment = []
positive_comment = []
neutral_comment = []
for i in tqdm(range(data.shape[0])):
    if data['Sentiment Score'][i] == 0 or data['Sentiment Score'][i] == 1:
        negative_comment.append(1)
        positive_comment.append(0)
        neutral_comment.append(0)
    elif data['Sentiment Score'][i] == 3 or data['Sentiment Score'][i] == 4:
        negative_comment.append(0)
        positive_comment.append(1)
        neutral_comment.append(0)
    else:
        negative_comment.append(0)
        positive_comment.append(0)
        neutral_comment.append(1)
data['Positive'] = positive_comment
data['Negative'] = negative_comment
data['Neutral'] = neutral_comment
